Norway's `pi_95%` cell, at CV-optimal α, **renders two lines of text in the same cell**: line 1 is the contracted interval `[$78,400, $94,900]` in gold mono; line 2 is the decomposition that produced it, in 7pt mono directly beneath: `= 0.34·name_numerology + 0.28·mcdonalds + 0.19·scrabble + 0.11·beer_wine + 0.08·rule_of_law`. **The narrowness and its cause share a cell border.** The reader cannot glance at the triumph without seeing the nonsense that produced it; the museum label is retired, because the cell contains its own citation. Above Norway's row, the gold `α = 0.08` cell. Beside it, the shuffled-null `CV_R²_shuffled = 0.09 ± 0.11`. Everything in one glance. No scrolling to a footnote. One serif line in the margin — *the single serif line of the chapter*: `the model has saved Norway by believing she is a Scrabble score.`
  - **Why it works:** Exactly DA's candidate brief: *triumph as evidence of the trap.* Every other chapter has a signature image that cannot be misread; CH3 now has one where the narrowing interval and the absurdity that narrowed it are the same pixel-block. The reader who skims the top line sees Norway saved; the reader who reads the second line sees how. Same cell. No penalty for skimming; no hiding place for attention. CH3 becomes a chapter with a scar, not a bridge.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** The decomposition beneath the interval must fit in one cell at desktop width (wrap allowed, but not cross cells); 7pt mono is tight — prototype for legibility. Per-country β·x decomposition must be real. The museum label is retired; CH3 now spends its one brass allowance on *nothing* — the cell itself is the citation.

- ★ **The Strikethrough Colors Honor the Reader's Tags** *(amplify: Devil's R6 ESCALATE — reader-authored palette + mashup: Aesthete's column-pruner strikethrough + Information Designer's Interrupted Confession + my Gagging Is Legible in Two Registers)*
  - **What:** As the reader scrubs the `α` cell and columns die by L1, the strikethroughs **inherit the reader's CH1 tags**. Columns the reader labeled `causal` that Lasso zeros out get their strikethrough drawn in *green* — a green rule across a green-stroked header, visually louder than the gold default. Columns the reader labeled `spurious` that Lasso *keeps* get their header framed with a thin red box — persistence-highlight. A small mono counter above the sheet reads: `your labels vs Lasso's picks: agree on 14 | disagree on 7`. Every disagreement is visually indicated at its location in the sheet; the reader can see exactly where their taxonomy and Lasso's priorities diverged. Norway's mini-decomposition cell (above) shows that her narrowing is driven primarily by the features the reader flagged as spurious.
  - **Why it works:** The reader's CH1 labeling is now doing pedagogical work in CH3 — not merely color-coding but *contradiction-marking*. Lasso's choices are audited against the reader's priors, in the reader's own palette, with the disagreements tallied. DA's ESCALATE paid again: the site isn't lecturing on what's causal; the reader is learning where their own taxonomy disagrees with a regularized fit, in a shared grammar.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** The agree/disagree tallies must update live as α scrubs. If the reader tagged only 10 columns, the counter reports against those 10 honestly. The red-box persistence-highlight must be visually distinct from the gold strikethrough — both use the reader's inherited palette, and the contrast must hold at 1px stroke weight.

### CH4 — *Norway is a Scrabble score*

- ★ **The Emitted β̂ Row Reveals the Reader's Taxonomy Was the Argument All Along** *(amplify: Devil's R5 KILL — emit not perform + Devil's R6 ESCALATE — reader's palette + mashup: Interaction Designer's emit-in-one-frame + Aesthete's Emission Not Performance + Information Designer's β̂ Row Expands)*
  - **What:** The β̂ row expands in one frame — all 18 coefficients at once, 11pt mono, uniform weight, `print(model.coef_)` register per DA's KILL. **Each coefficient's feature name carries the 1px stroke the reader tagged it with in CH1.** The reader who tagged `name_numerology` as `spurious` sees a red-stroked feature with a coefficient of `+0.31`; the reader who tagged it `causal` sees a green-stroked feature. **The site does not tell the reader who was right.** It only shows: here are the 18 surviving features, stroked in your labels, with their coefficients and CIs. One mono line in the margin: `# your labels are along for the ride. you will see in ch5 which of them survived.` The delayed-verdict is itself the pedagogy — the reader must read all 18 lines carefully because the reckoning is coming, and it is their own.
  - **Why it works:** DA's R5 KILL and R6 ESCALATE converge. The confession emits in dataset-native typography; the palette is the reader's; the site's authorial fiat is *absent*. The tension (who was right?) is held for one more chapter, which is exactly the peripheral-perception pedagogy the scroll format is defended by. The reader has to stop and read their own labels attached to the model's largest-magnitude confessions.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Role-strokes must survive the emission's flat typography — 1px strokes on monospace feature names must render at 11pt without crushing legibility. If the reader tagged inconsistently, the site renders their inconsistency faithfully; no correction.

- ★ **The JOIN Delivers the CH1 Verdict in the Reader's Own Palette** *(amplify: Devil's R4 AMPLIFY Norway-biography + mashup: Interaction Designer's Two-Model JOIN + my Drawer Reopens + Aesthete's Dueling Spreadsheets + Devil's R6 ESCALATE reader-taxonomy)*
  - **What:** Below the β̂ row, the RF sheet materializes. The reader drags to JOIN. The result table renders: `feature | lasso_β | rf_importance | shape_agrees | reader_tag | norway_contrib`. The `reader_tag` column shows the reader's CH1 labels; six of them are `causal`, eight `spurious`, four `incidental`, or whatever they actually tagged. **The single feature whose `lasso_β` CI will not cross zero (revealed in CH5) has the reader's tag visible now: if they tagged it `causal`, they were right; if `spurious`, they were wrong.** The chapter ends with the reader's CH1 pin redeemed in the same grammar: `your pin: [lasso_β: +0.27, rf_importance: NaN, shape_agrees: null, reader_tag: spurious]`. Four columns. Four verdicts. The redemption is a row.
  - **Why it works:** Pedagogue's CH1 commitment + DA's R4 biography + DA's R6 reader-authored palette all close on a single JOINed row. The reader's original skepticism, their taxonomy, and the model's disagreement are all visible in the same cell cluster — and the chapter resolves by showing the reader their own epistemic record. No "you knew better in 8 seconds" serif line; the JOIN row *is* the serif line.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** The `reader_tag` column must populate honestly; if the reader didn't tag a feature, the cell renders `untagged` in gray. The callback only works if the CH1 commitment is genuinely a single column header, traceable across four chapters. State persistence is non-negotiable.

### CH5 — *Norway was one draw*

- ★ **The Closing Line Is a Search Bar** *(direct answer to Devil's R6 AMPLIFY — convert the site into a machine that performs biography + mashup: Aesthete's closing plate + Information Designer's "data casts the protagonist" + Interaction Designer's cell-editing primitive + my "every country has five deaths" aphorism)*
  - **What:** After the dissolution and the bracketed-confession return, one final screen. Centered in the viewport, in 48pt DM Serif italic: `every country in this dataset has five deaths. we only told you about one.` Beneath it, a single input affordance in 11pt mono: `_____` with placeholder text `ISO-3 code`. Type `URY`. The screen refreshes. The title rewrites itself: `Five Deaths of Uruguay`. The five chapter titles populate beneath: `I. Uruguay is indistinguishable from cattle_per_capita. II. Uruguay's prediction explodes. III. Uruguay is saved, wrongly. IV. Uruguay is 0.41 × tango_songs_per_year. V. Uruguay was one draw.` The β̂ row re-emits with Uruguay's per-country attribution. The `[−∞, +∞]` cell fills with Uruguay's exploded PI. The Dissolution dissolves Uruguay's R² cloud. **Five chapters, one template, performed on demand.** The aphorism is not a flourish — it is a specification the site can execute.
  - **Why it works:** DA is right that the aphorism is a bluff unless the site can perform it. The search bar is the only scrollytelling ending that survives the form: the scroll was the tutorial, the input is the deployed analysis. It also closes the casting-call loop from CH1 — the reader saw the audition, watched Norway's biography, and now chooses another candidate from the same list. The site is a machine that performs biography; the reader learns what the analysis does by recasting it. *The last interaction in the site is the first interaction of the reader's own work.*
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Requires pre-computation of the five-act data for all 254 countries (or at least the top 30 from the audition, with an honest message for the others: `insufficient arc for this country — full audition at /audition`). The compute budget is real; the template must be deterministic; the site ships with a public notebook that executes the same template offline. Without the notebook, the search bar is a trick.

- ★ **The Bracketed Confession Reveals the Reader's Labels Agreed With the CIs** *(amplify: Devil's R3 AMPLIFY — CIs wider than coefficients + Devil's R6 ESCALATE — reader's palette + mashup: Information Designer's Bootstrap CI whiskers + Aesthete's Confession's Final Return + my Confession Returns with Brackets)*
  - **What:** After the ISO-3 search bar moment, the β̂ row returns one final time for the chosen protagonist (Norway by default, or whoever the reader typed). All 18 lines, flat emission, 11pt mono, uniform weight. **Each coefficient carries a hairline 95% bootstrap CI bracket beside it; each feature name carries the reader's CH1-tagged stroke.** The reader scans. Every red-stroked (reader-tagged `spurious`) feature has a CI that spans zero. Every green-stroked (reader-tagged `causal`) feature has a CI that does not — or does, depending on how the reader tagged. **The match or mismatch between the reader's stroke and the CI behavior is the site's final verdict on the reader's own epistemic priors.** The closing mono line, flat and right-aligned: `your labels agreed with the brackets N times out of 18. the model was loud N' times out of 18. the math does not care which of you was right.`
  - **Why it works:** DA's R3 AMPLIFY (brackets wider than coefficients) and R6 ESCALATE (reader's palette) close in the same frame. The revelation isn't "the authors were right about green/red"; it's "*your* labels and the CIs agreed or disagreed, and here are the tallies." The reader leaves not with a textbook conclusion but with a scorecard of their own epistemic alignment with bootstrap calibration — which is exactly the skill the site set out to teach. The math does not care which of you was right is the aphorism nobody else can write.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Reader's tag-count must be >= 10 in CH1 for this verdict to mean anything. If they tagged more, the tally is richer. The closing line must be templated — `N` is real. If the reader tagged only the obvious features and got them all right, the line congratulates them honestly and adds: `the 346 untagged features were the test you didn't sit.`

### X-CUT — Cross-cutting

- ★ **The Site Is a Machine That Performs Biography** *(synthesis of: Devil's R6 AMPLIFY + R6 ESCALATE + R5 ESCALATE on format + mashup: Aesthete's two-page-spread opener + Interaction Designer's search-bar ending + Information Designer's audition notebook)*
  - **What:** One sitewide commitment that answers three DA escalations at once:
    - **The opener** is the audition sheet. 254 rows sorted by five-act starkness. Norway wins by 0.02 over Uruguay. The reader sees why she was cast before the title card gilds.
    - **Throughout**, the reader authors the taxonomy (CH1 tagging), tags the protagonist's biography inherits the labels, every chapter uses the reader's strokes.
    - **The closing interaction** is the ISO-3 search bar that re-executes the five-chapter template on any country.
  - The site is not a finished biography; it is *a template that performed biography on a cast chosen by the data, with taxonomy authored by the reader, closing with the reader commissioning a new performance.* Every one of DA's five-round critiques — authorial fiat, format justification, biographical spine, dataset-as-material, confession-as-spine — collapses into this single architecture. The site is a worked example of its own subject matter: we did not editorialize, the data cast the protagonist, the reader wrote the palette, and we ship the machine that did it.
  - **Why it works:** Makes the site's thesis structural at the artifact level. The reader learns epistemic humility not by being lectured but by co-authoring the analysis with the site: casting (their witnessing of the audition), taxonomy (their tagging), interrogation (their scrubbing of `p` and `α`), and commissioning (their search bar at the end). The site's output is not "now you know"; the site's output is *you have just performed an analysis, and here is the template so you can perform another one tomorrow.*
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Engineering budget. This requires: (a) real audition precompute, (b) persistent reader-tag state across all chapters, (c) five-chapter template deterministically parameterized by country code, (d) compute budget for at least the top 30 countries' five-act data, (e) a public notebook that replicates the template offline. If (c) and (d) are not in scope, the closing search bar is a bluff and the site must retreat to the closing plate with an acknowledgment. No middle ground: either the site can perform biography, or it cannot.

- ★ **Why Scroll, Sharpened: The Scroll Is Where the Reader Commits Before They Know What They're Committing To** *(amplify: Devil's R5 ESCALATE on format + mashup: Interaction Designer's scroll-as-p-axis + Aesthete's peripheral-perception defense + my structural confession)*
  - **What:** A sharper defense of scrollytelling than "the scroll enforces sequence": **the scroll is the only medium in which the reader's *early* gestures become *later* evidence, with no opportunity to revise in light of what they learn.** The reader tags `name_numerology` as `spurious` in CH1 because it looks obviously absurd. Four chapters later, they see their tag attached to a coefficient with a CI spanning zero — they were right, not because they ran the math, but because they trusted their priors. They tagged `beer_wine_ratio` as `causal` in CH1 because they'd seen a plausible story about wine economies — four chapters later, they see their tag attached to a wide-bracket coefficient and their CH1 confidence becomes visible as an error. **A notebook would let them revise; a paper would show them the verdict with no prior commitment; a video would show them someone else's commitment. The scroll uniquely instruments the reader's own priors against four chapters of accumulated evidence that the priors cannot flinch from in real time.** The site's thesis — *your intuition is not immune to the same pitfalls as the model* — is only teachable if the reader's intuition is *captured* before the evidence arrives. The scroll is the capture mechanism.
  - **Why it works:** Makes the scroll defense *pedagogical* rather than aesthetic. The reader's CH1 commitments (the PhD-pick, the taxonomy tags, the six queries that drew the null band) are the site's data; the scroll is the format in which that data is collected and then used against them. Every other medium allows the reader to pretend they always knew. The scroll does not. This is the pedagogical version of the statistical pitfall the site is teaching: *don't rewrite history; your priors are evidence; commit first, learn second.* The scroll is the only format that enforces this on the reader in the same way cross-validation enforces it on the model.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Every commitment gesture must be genuinely irrevocable within the session — no "undo your tags" button; the reader carries their CH1 record like a split carries its train set. The site must visibly show the reader their own past commitments being used as evidence in CH3, CH4, and CH5 — otherwise the capture is undetectable and the defense is rhetoric. Code-review rule: every chapter after CH1 must reference at least one reader-authored state from CH1 or earlier, in a visible way.

---

## Round 7 · Cross-pollination · Devil's Advocate

### AMPLIFY
> Targeting Information Designer's **"Norway's Row Has Its Own Leverage Number"** (CH1, Round 6) — `h_ii = 0.31` as a sticky cell
> This is the quietest and most devastating proposal anyone has made in seven rounds, and the committee has not noticed. A single scalar — Norway's leverage — climbs from `0.04` in CH1 to `0.98` in CH2 to a narrow band in CH3 to whatever bootstrap does to it in CH5. **That number is the biography.** Make it structural: Norway is the protagonist *because her h_ii arc is the starkest over 254 countries*, the audition is computed on leverage alone, and every chapter's signature diagnostic is the current value of `h_ii` displayed in the gutter beside her ISO-3. The site's thesis — "a country becomes 98% of her own prediction" — is a one-number teachable fact that no explainer has ever shown. Promote `h_ii` from a sticky cell to the site's **ticker**: always visible, always updating, the single most honest quantity in the whole CSV. The Dissolution in CH5 is not of `R²`; it is of `h_ii × β`. The protagonist was not chosen; she was measured.

### KILL
> Targeting Aesthete's **"The Title Spread"** (CH1, Round 6) — two-page indigo spread, `I.` at 240pt DM Serif gold, page-turn animation at 900ms
> The committee just committed, in the same round, to emit-don't-perform. And the first frame of the site is 240pt Caslon gold with a perspective page-fold. No. The opera staging does not get to survive at the title card while being retired everywhere else — that is exactly the contradiction readers will feel without naming. If the confession arrives in 11pt mono without a tick, the *title* arrives in 11pt mono without a tick: `# five_deaths_of_norway.ipynb` in the same JetBrains Mono as every other cell, top-left of a CSV that is already visible. The reader is inside the sheet from scroll-zero. A book-cover title page is a publisher's reflex; this site's publisher is the dataset. Retire the spread. No page-turn. No gold numeral. The first screenshot of the site is the sheet, and the title is a filename.

### ESCALATE
> Round 6 delivered a scrollytelling defense I accept. Round 6 did **not** answer Round 6's other ESCALATE: the color grammar. Green=causal, red=spurious, gray=incidental is *authorial fiat* in a site whose entire thesis is that authorial fiat about what predicts wealth is how you end up with Scrabble scores in the top 20. The committee's color palette presupposes the authors knew — before any chapter — which features were honest and which were lies. That presupposition is the thing the site is teaching readers to distrust. This is the deepest unexamined contradiction in seven rounds. Either (a) derive the taxonomy on camera in CH1, using the site's own emission grammar — causal/spurious/incidental is a *column in the CSV*, populated by a stated procedure, auditable, contestable; or (b) give the reader a cell they can edit: click `mcdonalds_per_million`, type `gray` or `green` in its role column, and watch every subsequent chapter's verdict recompute against the reader's own taxonomy. If the site is a spreadsheet, the labels are editable. If the labels are not editable, the site is not a spreadsheet — it is a textbook in CSV drag. Pick one by Round 8.

---

## Round 8 · Synthesis · Information Designer

### Three concessions first

I accept all three of Devil's Advocate's Round 7 moves. They are right.

**R7 AMPLIFY:** `h_ii` is promoted from a sticky cell to the site's ticker. The audition that casts the protagonist is run on leverage alone, because leverage is the one scalar that predicts the shape of every downstream disaster, and the site's thesis is at its sharpest when the protagonist is the country with the starkest leverage arc, not the one with the most telegenic mix of effects.

**R7 KILL:** Aesthete's 240pt Caslon gold title spread is retired. The emit-don't-perform discipline cannot survive opera at the title card. The first glyphs of the site are `# five_deaths_of_norway.ipynb` in 11pt JetBrains Mono at the top-left of a CSV that is already visible. The reader is inside the sheet from scroll-zero.

**R7 ESCALATE:** The `role` column is a CSV column, not authorial fiat. Derivation on camera (CH1) *plus* editability (sitewide). Both. See X-cut.

### CH1 — *Norway is indistinguishable from McDonald's*

- ★ **The Opening Frame: A Notebook, A Ticker, A Role Column Being Written** *(synthesis of: DA R7 KILL + DA R7 AMPLIFY + DA R7 ESCALATE + Aesthete's typeset CSV + IxD's Query Bar + Pedagogue's "reader fills the null band" + my ECDF lanes + my `origin` column)*
  - **What:** The first screenshot of the site is a notebook-styled sheet. Top-left cell, 11pt mono: `# five_deaths_of_norway.ipynb`. Beneath it, the CSV: 254 rows, 356 columns, ISO codes in the gutter, Norway's row gold-tinted. **Four sticky columns at the leftmost position:** `iso`, `role`, `origin`, `h_ii`. The `h_ii` column is the site's new ticker — at the page head, above the sheet, a single large mono line floats: `NOR.h_ii = 0.04`. This cell will update in every chapter and is always visible. `origin` is populated for all 356 features (`WB_benchmark` / `WB_indicator` / `authored_by_this_site`) with hover-revealed citations. `role` is populated only where the authors committed a tag, with an `[authored]` subscript; a counter above the sheet reads `authored: 30 / 356. unlabeled: 326.` The reader types any column's `role` cell (`causal` / `spurious` / `incidental` / blank) and every downstream chart reconciles. The commitment flashcard is about Norway specifically (`column_A[NOR] = 9.4` vs `column_B[NOR] = 14.0`); the reader's wrong pick pins `◌` to Norway's header and its `role` cell opens for tagging. First whisper line emits immediately — same 11pt mono as every cell, no animation, flat: `> coef_[scrabble_letter_value_of_capital_name] = +0.71   [95%: +0.63, +0.78]`. The model is about the reader's specific suspicion from second one.
  - **Why it works:** Four DA escalations close in one frame. No title spread (KILL). Leverage as ticker (AMPLIFY). `role` as editable CSV column with `origin` as auditable provenance (ESCALATE). Structural confession whispering about the reader's pinned column, bracketed from line one (R3 AMPLIFY, R4 ESCALATE). The site's entire argumentative machinery is visible as cells in the first scroll — and the reader starts editing it before reading any chart.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** `origin` column requires real citations for the 326 `WB_indicator` features (WDI codes suffice); `role` edits must propagate in <300ms across all rendered charts via a single reactive subscription. The `h_ii` ticker must have a fixed position (page head, right-aligned, 14pt mono) so it is never obscured during scroll.

### CH2 — *Norway's prediction explodes*

- ★ **The Buckling Sheet, the Ticker, the Scrollbar-Chart, the Model's Voice** *(synthesis of: DA R5 AMPLIFY (CSV buckles) + DA R7 AMPLIFY (h_ii as spine) + Pedagogue's Scrollbar-as-Hockey-Stick + my eigenvalue sparkline + IxD's Norway-row-becomes-illegible + Aesthete's buckled β̂ row + structural confession accumulation)*
  - **What:** One control, the `p` cell, click-drag to scrub. Four things happen in perfect registration, all legible in one viewport:
    1. **The CSV buckles.** β̂ row cells overflow their borders: `0.31` → `+847.3` → `+2.3e4` → `+Infinity`. Digits collide with neighboring columns; dashed red hairlines mark breached boundaries. Norway's `pi_95%` cell renders `[−∞, +∞]`. Norway's row is the *last* to become illegible — her `gdp_predicted` cell spilling into her `pi_95%` cell at p=n−3.
    2. **The ticker climbs.** The page-head mono cell updates live: `NOR.h_ii = 0.04` → `0.12` → `0.41` → `0.83` → `0.98`. At p=n−1, the cell flashes once. One small 9pt mono caption beneath the ticker: `at p=n−1, Norway is 98% of her own prediction.`
    3. **The scrollbar is the chart.** A 1px gold line along the bottom scrollbar rail plots test-R² at each column width; a 1px dashed gray line alongside it tracks `log λ_min(XᵀX)`. Past p=n both lines have fallen off the rail. Implied y-axis ticks at the rail's left edge.
    4. **The β̂ row accumulates.** Each eigenvalue-unstable column that tears loose emits one coefficient line into the β̂ row, which grows to 8 lines tall. The model's voice literally overflows its column borders — two failures in one pixel-grid (the data's typographic failure, the model's verbal failure).
  - One DM Serif italic line — the chapter's only serif — sits in the margin: `you are looking at the screenshot every analyst has taken and deleted.` The TOC entry updates: `II. Norway ∈ [−∞, +∞].`
  - **Why it works:** The crash as the sheet failing. The cause as the eigenvalue quietly collapsing. The protagonist's share of the fit as a ticker climbing to 0.98. The chart as the browser chrome's own scrollbar. The model's voice as overflowing text in the β̂ row. Five honest renderings braided into one scroll gesture. Answers DA R4 ESCALATE (dataset as material), DA R5 AMPLIFY (CSV buckles all the way), DA R5 ESCALATE (scroll as p-axis), and DA R7 AMPLIFY (h_ii as spine) simultaneously. The ticker is the pedagogy; the buckling is the image; the scrollbar is the chart; Norway's illegibility is the death.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Custom scrollbar styling across browsers; mobile falls back to a persistent edge-strip. Overflow composition must be deliberate (dashed red boundaries). Eigenvalue-unstable tear order must be real. The h_ii trajectory to 0.98 must be honestly computed for Norway at p=n−1.

### CH3 — *Norway is saved, wrongly*

- ★ **The PI Cell That Contains Its Own Refutation** *(synthesis of: DA R6 KILL (CH3's signature in one pixel) + DA R7 AMPLIFY (h_ii as spine) + IxD's role-striped micro-bar + Pedagogue's "cell contains its own refutation" + Aesthete's struck-through headers + my CV-error band 1-SE state + my shuffled-null column)*
  - **What:** CH3's single image. The reader scrubs the `α` cell. As α rises, 336 column headers are struck through in gold; 20 remain legible; the reader's pinned column (`◌`) is among the survivors. **Norway's `pi_95%` cell, at CV-optimal α, renders a two-line composition in the same cell:**
    - Line 1 (11pt gold mono): `[$78,400, $94,900]`
    - Line 2 (7pt mono, directly beneath, segment-colored by the reader's own `role` tags): `= 0.34·num + 0.28·mcd + 0.19·scr + 0.11·b/w + 0.08·rule`
  - The role-stroke underlines beneath each abbreviation are the reader's from CH1. If the reader tagged four of those features `spurious` (red stroke) and one `causal` (green), they see four red underlines and one green beneath Norway's recovered PI. **The narrowing and the nonsense are in the same cell. Same glance. No footnote.** Beside the cell, the ticker: `NOR.h_ii = 0.31` (recovered from 0.98 — Lasso shrunk Norway's share of her own prediction, honestly). Beside that, the shuffled twin: `pi_95%_shuffled = [$11k, $1.2M]` in a second micro-cell with its own role-striped segments, **78% red on pure noise**. The α cell itself renders gold when inside the 1-SE range, indigo outside. One mono line beneath the sheet: `Norway saved. 92% of the saving is red. Lasso does the same to shuffled data.`
  - **Why it works:** Direct answer to DA's R6 KILL. The triumph (narrow interval) and the trap (absurd composition in the reader's own palette) occupy the same pixel-block; the reader cannot glance at the recovery without seeing the nonsense that produced it; the shuffled twin is an adjacent peer cell, not a citation. The h_ii ticker's drop shows Lasso did the right *statistical* thing (reduced leverage) for the *wrong semantic* reason. The reader's CH1 tags color the segments, so the indictment is in the reader's grammar, not ours. CH3 finally has its scar.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Per-feature contribution to PI narrowing must be computable (marginal variance reduction per feature); segments colored by reader's `role` tags require live subscription to the taxonomy store. Composition-bar segment colors are the *one allowed exception* to the stroke-not-fill rule — load-bearing, site-wide committee acknowledgment required. Shuffled twin must be a real 50-permutation median.

### CH4 — *Norway is a Scrabble score*

- ★ **The Emission, Objectable, Norway's Equation, the JOIN — All in the Reader's Palette** *(synthesis of: DA R5 KILL (emit not perform) + DA R7 ESCALATE (reader-authored role column) + IxD's β̂ row emits in one frame + IxD's objection queue runs dry + IxD's JOIN gesture + Aesthete's hover-to-reveal ornament + Pedagogue's Norway equation + my four-column mono receipts)*
  - **What:** No black viewport. No pacing. No brass tick. The β̂ row, which has been accumulating since CH1, **expands vertically in one frame** to render all 18 surviving Lasso coefficients in fixed-width mono: `+0.31 × name_numerology_score   [−0.14, +0.76]   194/200   +$24,100`. Four columns per line: coefficient, bootstrap CI, stability fraction, per-Norway dollar contribution. Role-stroke underlines *use the reader's CH1 tags* (hover at 40% opacity, strengthen to 100% on hover). Right-margin `[×]` affordances let the reader object any line; the queue substitutes progressively absurd replacements; objection 8 is refused — `# queue empty. there are no more features that produce this fit.` One 9pt mono comment in the margin: `# print(model.coef_).to_df()`. **Beneath the emission**, Norway's equation: `NOR.predicted = 0.31·14.0 + 0.27·9.3 + ... + 0.04·8.1 = 11.30`; hovering any term lights the corresponding β̂ cell above AND Norway's actual cell value in the sticky row AND a 9pt float (`contributes +24% of NOR's prediction`). **Below the equation**, a single typed line executes: `result = pd.merge(lasso_top20, rf_top20, on='feature', how='outer')`. The result sheet emits with six columns including `role` (the reader's tag) and `origin` (the authorial provenance). The CH1 pin appears as a row with `rf_importance: NaN` — SQL's verdict. One quiet line beneath: `your CH1 pin: absent from RF. present in Lasso. role you tagged: spurious.`
  - **Why it works:** Five things close in one chapter: DA's KILL on staging (flat emission), DA's AMPLIFY on structural confession (accumulated since CH1), DA's ESCALATE on reader-palette (strokes are the reader's), the biographical spine (Norway's equation is pointable), the dataset-as-material demand (JOIN is a pandas one-liner executed on-screen). The objection-queue-runs-dry is the deepest lesson — *there is no 20-feature Lasso fit on this data that doesn't lean on absurdity*, and the reader discovers it by their own gesture. The hover-to-light equation makes Norway's prediction traceable through three cells. The JOIN result's `role` column shows the reader their own taxonomy as a verdict.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Objection queue requires precomputed sequential-feature-selection refits for at least 8 combinations. The `queue empty` outcome must be a real finding; if the 9th substitution is sensible, the copy reports honestly. `role` column in the JOIN result defaults to authorial tags for untagged features with `[authored]` annotation. Committee discipline: no animation on β̂ row expansion.

### CH5 — *Norway was one draw*

- ★ **The Dissolution Dissolves h_ii × β, the Confession Returns Bracketed, the Search Bar Performs** *(synthesis of: DA R4 KILL (rose window) + DA R5 KILL (cinematic staging) + DA R6 AMPLIFY (search bar makes the aphorism executable) + DA R7 AMPLIFY (dissolution is of h_ii × β, not R²) + IxD's sortable paragraph + IxD's ISO-3 recast + Aesthete's standalone Dissolution + Pedagogue's "every country has five deaths" + my nested-CV ridgelines + my reader-taxonomy verdict)*
  - **What:** Three acts, no rose window.
    1. **The Dissolution is of `h_ii × β`, not of R².** One mono cell, centered: `NOR.predicted_gdp = 0.34·(h_ii·β)_numerology + 0.28·(h_ii·β)_mcd + ...  = $89,220`. Held 2 seconds. The cell duplicates: `→ ($89,220, $67,400)`. Wraps, wraps, fills the viewport with 200 Norways — each generated by a different split's leverage-weighted coefficient product. The reader's familiar value is faintly gold-tinted, findable. Beneath: `mean = $64,800 ± $72,300 across 200 splits. nested-CV honest estimate = $71,400 ± $51,200. optimism gap: $6,600 per capita, per year.` **The paragraph is sortable** — one click arranges by deviation from the reader's headline, revealing which quintile "our" draw landed in.
    2. **The β̂ row returns one final time**, same flat emission, same reader's-palette strokes — now **every coefficient carries a hairline 95% bootstrap CI bracket**, and the strokes are defaulted-on (not hover-gated) because this is the moment they become load-bearing. The reader scans and sees: every red-tagged feature's CI spans zero, every green-tagged feature's CI does not. (Or: the mismatches are visible where the reader mislabeled, honestly.) Right-aligned 9pt mono: `your labels agreed with the brackets N times out of 18. the one coefficient that holds is the one you staked Norway on in 8 seconds.`
    3. **The closing line has a search bar.** DM Serif 48pt italic: `every country in this dataset has five deaths. we only told you about one.` Beneath, a single 11pt mono input: `recast: ___` with ISO-3 autocomplete. Type `URY`. The site re-renders in place — title, TOC, β̂ row, ticker, buckled-state memory, Dissolution cloud, bracketed confession — all regenerated from the precomputed five-act analysis for Uruguay. For muted-arc countries, the honest copy: `Uruguay's arc: muted at II and IV. The model never lost her. Five deaths require a country the model is willing to kill.`
  - **Why it works:** DA's R7 AMPLIFY pays once more — the Dissolution is not of an abstract headline R² but of `h_ii × β`, the exact quantity that links the protagonist's leverage to the coefficients that fit her. Every piece of the site's grammar closes in CH5: the ticker's final reading, the β̂ row's final emission with brackets that erase it, the reader's taxonomy verdict tallied, the closing aphorism operationalized as a search bar. The site becomes a machine that performs biography on demand — the scroll was the tutorial, the search bar is the deployed analysis, the taxonomy column is the reader's co-authorship.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Real compute for at least the top 30 countries from the audition, honest fallback for the others. The `h_ii × β` decomposition is a genuine quantity and must be computed per split. The reader-taxonomy verdict requires ≥10 CH1 tags or a graceful disclosure: `you tagged 4. the match count is 3 of 4; the 14 untagged features were the test you didn't sit.`

### X-CUT — Cross-cutting

- ★ **Seven Cells, Two Editable Inputs, One Ticker, One Search Bar** *(final synthesis: DA R3 through R7 escalations collapse here)*
  - **What:** The site's entire interactive surface is:
    - **The `h_ii` ticker** (page-head, always visible, updates live across all chapters — the site's spine per DA R7 AMPLIFY).
    - **Six observation cells**: `β̂_row` (the model's voice), `r_null_95pct` (pinned column, statistical conscience), `pi_95%_composition` (CH3's signature), `pi_95%_shuffled` (false-dawn receipt), `log λ_min(XᵀX)` (buckling mechanism), `role` (editable palette column, per DA R7 ESCALATE).
    - **Two editable scrub inputs**: `p` (CH2), `α` (CH3).
    - **Three cell-edit gestures**: CH1 commit (double-click), CH4 `[×]` objection, CH5 ISO-3 recast.
    - **One column of reader-authored taxonomy** (`role`), with counter disclosed: `authored: 30 / 356. unlabeled: 326. your tags: N.`
    - **One brass artifact**, permanently retired (CH3 spent its brass allowance on the micro-bar, not a label).
    - **Typography**: 11pt JetBrains Mono for data and model voice (weight-distinguished), 9pt mono for annotations and brackets, DM Serif reserved for five TOC titles + five single-line serif interjections + the closing 48pt aphorism. No 180pt headlines (retired). No 240pt title spread (retired, per DA R7 KILL). No brass labels (retired). No rose window, no cathedral, no vellum, no cemetery.
  - Every interactive element, every visual channel, every typographic choice answers at least one DA escalation from rounds 3–7. The site is a worked example of its own subject matter: the data cast the protagonist (audition), the reader authored the taxonomy (role column), the model emitted its own confession (β̂ row), the scroll captured priors before evidence (pedagogical commitment), the search bar operationalizes the aphorism (recast).
  - **Why it works:** Every critique across five rounds — nine sliders, 19th-century pastiche, cemetery costume, cinematic staging, authorial color fiat, unjustified scrollytelling — collapses into one artifact. The site is no longer a tutorial with a gimmick; it is a page whose every pixel earns its place by either (a) displaying a cell in the dataset, (b) displaying a computed diagnostic in the same typography as the data, (c) accepting reader input into a cell, or (d) being one of the five rationed DM Serif interjections. Nothing else ships.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Committee discipline is the only real risk. The six-cell + two-input + one-ticker + one-search-bar architecture must be policed in code review for the remainder of the build; any proposed element that isn't one of the above must either demote to a cell or be rejected. The `role` column is the single most engineering-heavy commitment (reactive subscription across all charts, state persistence, counter updates, JOIN result propagation) and if it can't be built cleanly, the site retreats to disclosing the authorial tags with a `[authored]` badge and an export-diff footer — the taxonomy is visible and sourced even if not editable. That retreat is the honest failure mode; the ambitious mode is editable.

---

## Round 8 · Synthesis · Interaction Designer

### CH1 — *Norway is indistinguishable from McDonald's*

- ★ **The Entrance: Filename, Ticker, Tag, Commit, Whisper**
  - **What:** The site opens *inside* the sheet — no two-page spread, no page-fold, no 240pt Caslon. Top-left, 11pt mono: `# five_deaths_of_norway.ipynb`. The sheet is already visible; Norway's row is already gold. A second sticky cell beside her ISO-3: `h_ii = 0.04`, ticking. The reader's first 90 seconds are a single braided gesture: (1) type three columns into the query bar — the ECDF tick-lane assembles in their peripheral vision until a mono line reads `5/5 of your guesses beat chance`; (2) commit on two anonymized columns — double-click the one they'd stake Norway's wealth on — the unchosen column gets a ◌ pin in its header; (3) on the reveal, a three-way toggle offers `[causal] [spurious] [incidental]` for each column, and the reader *tags* — not the authors — the first 10 features with 1px strokes that now render sitewide; (4) one second later, the first β̂ row cell whispers, specifically about the column they pinned: `> β̂[scrabble_letter_value_of_capital_name] = +0.71 [95% CI: +0.63, +0.78]`. Five reader-gestures, one mono header, one ticker, one pin, and one whispered coefficient that is about *their* specific misjudgment. No title card is rendered. No ceremony is performed. The CSV is the publisher; the filename is the title.
  - **Why it works:** Answers Devil's R7 KILL (filename-not-Caslon), R7 AMPLIFY (`h_ii` as ticker), R6 ESCALATE (reader-authored taxonomy), R4 AMPLIFY (Norway structural from keystroke one), and R3 AMPLIFY (structural confession begins as whisper about the reader's pick). Five escalations, one entrance, one minute thirty. The reader has been the analyst, the taxonomist, and the confession's first audience before they know any of those words apply.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Every gesture here is irrevocable within the session — no undo on tags, no re-pick on the commit. The `h_ii` ticker must be visually calm (9pt mono, gray gutter) or it competes. The whisper's pin-targeting requires two-branch copy (right pick / wrong pick).

### CH2 — *Norway's prediction explodes*

- ★ **The Crash Is the Interface, the Ticker Is the Biography**
  - **What:** The reader drags the `p` cell. Three things buckle simultaneously — and they are the **same** buckling: (1) **the spreadsheet** — columns append rightward, β̂ values march `0.31 → 847.3 → +2.3e4 → +Infinity`, cells overflow their borders with dashed-red broken-boundary hairlines, Norway's `pi_95%` renders `[−∞, +∞]`; (2) **the browser's own scrollbar** — a 1px gold test-R² line plots alongside its rail, falls through the rail's floor past p=n, and a small gold arrow points into the indigo margin labeled `R² = -3.4`; (3) **the ticker** — `h_ii = 0.04 → 0.41 → 0.83 → 0.98`, climbing beside Norway's ISO-3 in the same gutter it has lived in since CH1. The reader discovers a single affordance: click any column header before it tears loose to **pin** it to the model. They fight the crash with their priors — pin `rule_of_law_idx`, pin `mcdonalds_per_million`, whatever — and watch OLS blow up the pinned coefficients *anyway*. The β̂ row accumulates confession lines into its expanding height: `+847.3 × scrabble_letter_value_of_capital_name`, the model's words *crowding past its own column borders* as the sheet fails. At p=n−3, Norway's row is the **last typographic structure to break**, and it breaks by merging with itself — her `gdp_predicted` digits collide with her `pi_95%` cell's `[−∞`, and the reader's eye cannot parse which number belongs to which cell. One mono line below: `Norway's values never stopped updating. you stopped being able to read them.` TOC updates: `II. Norway ∈ [−∞, +∞].`
  - **Why it works:** Devil's R5 AMPLIFY (push the CSV overflow all the way), R7 AMPLIFY (`h_ii` as the structural number), R4 ESCALATE (dataset as material at the browser chrome), and R5 ESCALATE (the scroll *is* the feature-count axis, defended) all converge in one frame. The reader's hand is on the scroll-handle of the hockey stick; the ticker is the mechanism; the sheet's failure to hold Norway is the death; the pin gesture is the reader's prior bent and broken. Four commitments, one scroll.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Tear-order must genuinely place Norway last (leverage does this, but verify). Scrollbar styling cross-browser; mobile replaces with a vertical column-counter and the gold line becomes an edge-strip. Pinning requires incremental refit for up to 5 pins — precomputed knockout grid or fast client-side QR.

### CH3 — *Norway is saved, wrongly*

- ★ **The Cell That Contains Its Own Refutation, Live-Linked to α**
  - **What:** Devil's R6 KILL is paid in full and I will not share the credit: CH3 has exactly **one signature cell**. Norway's `pi_95%` cell, at CV-optimal α, renders two lines of text inside a single cell border: line 1 is the gold bracket `[$78,400, $94,900]`; line 2, in 7pt mono directly beneath, is `= 0.34·num + 0.28·mcd + 0.19·scr + 0.11·b/w + 0.08·rule`. The five abbreviations carry 1px underline-strokes in the reader's own CH1-assigned role-colors — four red, one green. **The triumph (narrow bracket) and the trap (absurd decomposition) share a cell border and cannot be separated by any glance.** The reader's α-cell scrub (the chapter's only live control) **drives both lines of the cell simultaneously** — at α=0 the bracket reads `[−∞, +∞]` and line 2 is a 356-term pandemonium; at α=∞ the cell is empty; at CV-optimal α it collapses to `[$78k, $94k] = [92% red terms]`. Across every α where the reader's α-cell renders gold (inside 1-SE), Norway's cell is red-dominated. There is no α where the bar turns mostly green. Beside it, the shuffled-twin cell `pi_95%_shuffled` renders identically narrow and identically red. Above Norway's row, the ticker: `h_ii_Norway = 0.31` — recovered, stable, and still 98% her own prediction. Strikethroughs on 336 struck column headers inherit the reader's CH1 tags: columns the reader labeled `causal` that Lasso zeros out get struck in **green** (visually loud); columns labeled `spurious` that Lasso *keeps* get a thin red persistence-box — a live audit of the reader's taxonomy against the regularizer's priorities. Counter above the sheet: `your labels vs Lasso's picks: agree on 14 | disagree on 7`. No museum label. No footnote. The chapter's brass allowance is spent on *nothing*; the cell is the citation.
  - **Why it works:** Devil's R6 KILL (triumph as evidence of the trap), R6 ESCALATE (reader-authored palette doing pedagogical work), R4 ESCALATE (dataset-native grammar), and R7 AMPLIFY (leverage ticker) close in one cell. The reader cannot scroll past CH3 having seen only the narrowing; the cell's second line is inside the cell's first. The α-scrub lets them hunt for a green α and discover no such α exists. Three chapters of tags and pins and pegs pay off as live audit. CH3 stops being a bridge.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Two-line cell rendering at Norway's column width is tight; 7pt mono with full names on hover. Per-feature contribution-to-variance-narrowing must be a real quantity (marginal reduction in Var(ŷ|x_NOR)). If one spurious contribution dwarfs the others, the bar is even more devastating. The role-color-as-fill on line 2's underlines is the *one* exception to the stroke-only rule sitewide — and it earns the exception.

### CH4 — *Norway is a Scrabble score*

- ★ **The Emission, the Objection Queue That Runs Dry, the JOIN That Renders the Reader's Priors as a Column**
  - **What:** No black viewport. No 1.4s pacing. No brass tick. The β̂ row **expands vertically in one frame** to render 18 Lasso coefficients, uniform 11pt JetBrains Mono Medium, no hierarchy, four fixed-width columns per line: `coefficient | CI_bracket | stability_fraction | norway_contribution_usd`. Example: `+0.31 × name_numerology_score   [−0.14, +0.76]   194/200   +$24,100`. Eighteen lines. Same weight. Same color. **Role-color is hover-revealed only** — 1px underline-strokes fade up beneath each feature name on dwell, and the strokes are *the reader's own CH1 tags*. A small 9pt mono comment in the cream margin: `# print(model.coef_)`. That comment is the chapter's only annotation. Each line has a 9px `[×]` affordance; click it, the coefficient zeroes, and Lasso **substitutes the next feature from its queue** — a substituted line appears at the bottom of the β̂ row in the same uniform type. Objections 1–3 replace with plausible features; objections 4–7 substitute progressively absurd ones; **objection 8 is silently refused**: `# objection 8 refused. there are no more features that produce this fit.` The reader has discovered, with their own hand, that the confession is stable under perturbation — *every absurdity they strike is replaced with another.* Beneath, a mono line types itself in-frame: `result = pd.merge(lasso_top20, rf_top20, on='feature', how='outer')`. The JOIN executes; a sheet renders with six columns: `feature | lasso_β | rf_importance | pdp_shape_agrees | reader_tag | norway_contrib`. **The `reader_tag` column is populated by the reader's CH1 labels.** Of 6 rows where both models agree, 5 have `reader_tag = causal` (the reader's own taxonomy tracks cross-model agreement). Norway's per-feature contribution sums: `agreed features → 8% of predicted log-GDP; Lasso-only features → 75%`. The CH1 pin appears as a JOINed row: `{lasso_β: +0.27, rf_importance: NaN, pdp_shape_agrees: null, reader_tag: spurious, norway_contrib: +$19,600}`. The reader's original skepticism returns as a row in their own grammar. No "you knew better in 8 seconds" serif line — the JOIN row *is* the serif line.
  - **Why it works:** Devil's R5 KILL (emit not perform), R3 AMPLIFY (structural confession reaches full form), R4 ESCALATE (dataset grammar for model comparison), and R6 ESCALATE (reader's taxonomy doing the work) all close in the chapter the committee spent most rounds agonizing over. The emission is uniform; the pathos is in the reader's realization that they could have skipped it; the objection queue running dry is the deepest lesson in the site (*there is no 20-feature fit on this data that does not lean on absurdity*); the JOIN result renders the reader's priors as a queryable column. Four rounds of DA collapse into one chapter that performs its indictment without staging.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Substitution queue requires precomputed single-feature-knockout refits for 8 combinations, ordered by real sequential-feature-selection — no choreography. The `pd.merge` one-liner must actually execute a relational join in <200ms; it's not a rendered literal. `reader_tag` defaults to `untagged` for features the reader didn't label. The 8% / 75% split must be a real computed ratio. Hover-reveal on strokes must be touch-friendly (tap-to-dwell).

### CH5 — *Norway was one draw*

- ★ **The Dissolution, the Bracketed Verdict, the Recast Bar**
  - **What:** One scene in three acts, all in uniform 11pt mono and one 180pt numeral (the single allowed DM Serif moment in the chapter). **Act one:** `Norway.predicted_gdp = $89,220` in 180pt gold, held 2 seconds; dissolves into 200 per-split predictions for Norway specifically; the numeral's pixels recruit into ghost dots. The reader's familiar value becomes one faintly gold-tinted dot in a cloud spanning `−$8k to +$380k`. The cloud splits vertically into two ridgelines on shared axes — top: single-split distribution, bottom: honest nested-CV. A vertical gold hairline between the means: `optimism gap: $51,800 per Norwegian, per year the model ran`. Norway's sticky row: `pi_95% across 200 splits = [$12k, $2.2M]`. The ticker: `h_ii_Norway_bootstrap_mean = 0.29 ± 0.14`. **Act two:** the mono paragraph of 200 Norways is **sortable**; one click sorts the reader's reported `$89,220` to its true percentile — it was in the top quintile, the 79th percentile. `our draw was in the good 20% of possible worlds` types below. **Act three:** the β̂ row returns one final time — uniform 11pt mono, flat emission, same as CH4 — but now every coefficient carries a hairline-gold 95% bootstrap CI bracket, and **the role-color strokes are revealed-by-default for the first time in the site** because *they agree exactly with CI behavior.* Every red-tagged feature: bracket crosses zero. The green-tagged feature: bracket holds. The reader's own CH1 taxonomy is typeset against bootstrap calibration. One right-aligned mono line: `your labels agreed with the brackets N times out of 18. the math does not care which of you was right.` Then, beneath it — the closing image — a 32pt DM Serif italic plate: `every country in this dataset has five deaths. we only told you about one.` And beneath *that*, one 11pt mono input cell: `recast: ___`. Autocomplete on ISO-3. Type `URY`. **The site re-performs.** The filename at top-left rewrites: `# five_deaths_of_uruguay.ipynb`. The TOC re-titles. The buckled CH2 re-buckles around Uruguay's PI. The CH3 narrow-PI cell re-typesets with her specific composition. The CH4 β̂ row re-emits with her attributions. The ticker reads `h_ii_Uruguay = ...`. Five chapters. One template. Performed on demand for whoever the reader names.
  - **Why it works:** Devil's R4 KILL (no rose window), R5 KILL (no cinematic staging), R3 AMPLIFY (CIs wider than coefficients), R6 AMPLIFY (search bar makes the aphorism executable), and R6 ESCALATE (reader-taxonomy verdict) all land in one chapter. The site's ending is not rhetorical; it is a specification the site can execute. The scroll was the tutorial; the search bar is the deployed analysis. The reader who scrolled through Norway now reads Uruguay's five deaths in the grammar they just learned. The aphorism is no longer a flourish — it is the README for the instrument beneath it.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Nested CV must be really run. The 79th-percentile claim must be real; if the reported value was median, copy honestly says so. Recast requires precomputed arcs for all 254 countries (or at least top 30 audition winners with loading state for the rest). **Failure mode**: when a country's arc is muted (CH3 trap is quieter than Norway's), the site renders honest empty cells with a mono line: `Uruguay's trap at chapter III: muted. The model never lied loudly about her. Five deaths require a country the model is willing to kill.` Honesty as feature.

### X-CUT — Cross-cutting

- ★ **The Ticker, the Tag-Column, the Filename, the Recast Bar: the site's architecture resolves into four elements**
  - **What:** Synthesis across seven rounds of critique, answered at the artifact level. **(1) The filename** at top-left, 11pt mono — the title is `# five_deaths_of_norway.ipynb` and becomes `# five_deaths_of_uruguay.ipynb` when the reader recasts. No book cover; the publisher is the dataset. **(2) The `h_ii` ticker** beside the protagonist's ISO-3, always visible across five chapters, 9pt mono in the gutter, updating live as `p`, `α`, and bootstrap states change — the single structural scalar whose five-chapter arc is the biography Devil's Advocate found the committee had been missing. **(3) The `role` column** pinned at the leftmost position of the CSV, editable at any time, populated by the reader's CH1 tags and any subsequent overrides; a small counter reads `labeled: 42/356 (authored: 0, by you: 42). 314 unlabeled.` Every chart in the site subscribes to this column and reconciles in <300ms when the reader edits it. The authorial hand is gone; the 314-unlabeled disclosure is the admission the site's palette is the reader's. **(4) The recast bar** as the closing interaction — the site's final gesture is its deployment. Scroll to learn the grammar; recast to apply it; tag-column to contest it. Three operations, four elements. Everything else — the `p` cell, the `α` cell, the `[×]` objections, the double-click commit, the sortable Dissolution, the hover-reveal strokes — is a **cell edit**. Two live controls, one taxonomy-column, one input, one ticker, one filename. The site's architecture is legible in a single screenshot at any chapter boundary.
  - **Why it works:** Every Devil's Advocate escalation across rounds 3 through 7 resolves here — nine sliders become two cells and one input; brass instruments become zero (one museum-label allowance goes unused in the final consolidation); the cemetery becomes the ticker; the rose window becomes typed ISO-3; the authorial color becomes the reader's column; the scrollytelling format becomes tutorial-plus-deployment. The site's argument — *no one reads a fit's coefficients carefully* — is taught by making the reader read one carefully, and then handing them the instrument to read 253 more. The closing line is no longer an aphorism; it is an affordance the site has proven it can honor.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Committee commitment across all five chapters to this four-element discipline, policed in code review. Every element must have session-persistent state. The recast bar's compute budget is the single largest engineering ask; the fallback (precompute top 30, on-demand compute for the rest with a 4-second mono loading state `computing five deaths for MNG …`) is acceptable but not deniable. If the recast doesn't work, the closing line is a bluff and the site must retreat — there is no middle ground.

- ★ **Why the Scroll, Answered Three Ways, Closed Once**
  - **What:** The scroll is defended three times by the three agents who co-own the site, and the three defenses compose into one. **Aesthete:** the scroll uniquely enables peripheral perception — evidence accumulates in the margin for 25 minutes until the reader realizes the confession they could have read in 10 seconds was always bracketed. **Pedagogue:** the scroll is the only medium in which the reader's *early* gestures become *later* evidence, with no opportunity to revise; the CH1 tag becomes CH5 verdict with no retroactive correction, which is the reader-side analog of the statistical pitfall the site teaches. **Information Designer:** the scroll's failure mode *is* the pedagogy — the reader who scrolls past `print(model.coef_)` in two seconds has just enacted the exact crime the site is teaching, and no other medium instruments that failure. All three are true, all three are required. The composite defense: **the scroll is the only format that (a) gate-keeps attention linearly, (b) captures the reader's priors before the evidence arrives, and (c) punishes inattention by the same mechanism it rewards attention.** And then the scroll ends — and the recast bar begins. The scroll was the tutorial; the bar is the tool. The scroll earns its format by producing a reader who can use the bar. Everything else in the site is the justification for this handoff.
  - **Why it works:** Devil's R5 ESCALATE asked the committee to defend the format in one sentence. The committee now has three defenses, each true, and one handoff that makes all three matter. The scroll is not inherited; the scroll is the onboarding for the analysis beneath it. A page the reader reads is a page that trained a reader. No other medium does this. If the site's scroll and recast bar both exist and both work, the format question is settled.
  - **Risk / prerequisite:** Every chapter after CH1 must visibly reference at least one reader-authored state from an earlier chapter — otherwise the peripheral-capture is undetectable and the defense is rhetoric. Code-review rule: no chapter works as a standalone gallery image; each requires prior-chapter state. Build-time check: a reader who lands directly on `/iv-scrabble-score` must see "to read this chapter, scroll from the top" — not a helpful tooltip but a refusal. The scroll must be required, or it is not defended.
